Clicking on a transaction reminder will display a window where you can automatically record the transaction.\r\n\r\n∞ ONLINE BANKING\r\nMoneydance can automatically download transactions and send payments online from hundreds of financial institutions. It learns how to categorize and clean up downloaded transactions. Send online payments, for banks that support them, directly from scheduled transaction notifications.
